(*****************************************************************************************

 The comprehension functor of setgroupoids

 In this file, we define the comprehension functor that sends isofibrations on some
 setgroupoid [Γ] to a functor into [Γ]. Since we represent isofibrations using displayed
 categories, we use the total category and the projection of a displayed category. We
 also show that this functor is Cartesian. To do so, we verify that the chosen lifts, which
 are given by reindexing, are sent to pullback squares.

 Content
 1. The total category of an isofibration
 2. The comprehension functor
 3. Some transport lemmas that we need
 4. The comprehension functor is Cartesian
 5. Comprehension for split isofibrations

 *****************************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.
[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

  (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid)

∏ x : cat_of_setgroupoid,
disp_cat_isofib x
→ disp_codomain cat_of_setgroupoid
    (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid x)
(λ Fob : ∏ x : cat_of_setgroupoid,
         disp_cat_isofib x
         → disp_codomain cat_of_setgroupoid
             (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid x),
 ∏ (x y : cat_of_setgroupoid) (xx : disp_cat_isofib x)
 (yy : disp_cat_isofib y)
 (f : cat_of_setgroupoid ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 xx -->[ f] yy
 → Fob x xx -->[
   # (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid) f] Fob y yy)
  ?pr1

  
∏ x : cat_of_setgroupoid,
disp_cat_isofib x
→ disp_codomain cat_of_setgroupoid
    (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid x)
 exact (λ (G : setgroupoid)
             (D : disp_cat_isofib G),
           total_set_groupoid D
           ,,
           pr1_category _).
  
(λ Fob : ∏ x : cat_of_setgroupoid,
         disp_cat_isofib x
         → disp_codomain cat_of_setgroupoid
             (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid x),
 ∏ (x y : cat_of_setgroupoid) (xx : disp_cat_isofib x)
 (yy : disp_cat_isofib y)
 (f : cat_of_setgroupoid ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 xx -->[ f] yy
 → Fob x xx -->[
   # (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid) f] Fob y yy)
  (λ (G : setgroupoid) (D : disp_cat_isofib G),
   total_set_groupoid D,, pr1_category (pr11 D))
 
G₁, G₂: setgroupoid
D₁: disp_cat_isofib G₁
D₂: disp_cat_isofib G₂
F: G₁ ⟶ G₂
FF: D₁ -->[ F] D₂
total_functor (pr1 FF)
· pr2 (total_set_groupoid D₂,, pr1_category (pr11 D₂)) =
pr2 (total_set_groupoid D₁,, pr1_category (pr11 D₁))
· # (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid) F

    exact (total_functor_commute_eq (pr1 FF)).
Defined.

(gg : yy -->[ g] zz),

(** * 3. Some transport lemmas that we need *)
Definition transportf_functor_disp_ob
           {C₁ C₂ : category}
           {D : disp_cat C₂}
           {F₁ F₂ : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
           (p : F₁ = F₂)
           {x : C₁}
           (xx : D (F₁ x))
  : D (F₂ x)
  := transportf D (maponpaths (λ (F : _ ⟶ _), F x) p) xx.


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportb D (path_functor_ob p x)
  (transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx) = xx


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportb D (path_functor_ob p x)
  (transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx) = xx

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
xx = xx

  apply idpath.
Defined.


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportf D (path_functor_ob p x) xx =
transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂

p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportf D (path_functor_ob p x) xx =
transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx

xx = xx

  apply idpath.
Defined.

D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
# F₂ f] transportf_functor_disp_ob p yy

D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)

ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf_functor_disp_ob (idpath F₁) xx -->[
# F₁ f] transportf_functor_disp_ob (idpath F₁) yy

  exact ff.
Defined.


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf_functor_disp_mor p ff =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ y ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z] transportf_functor_disp_ob p yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left p f)
  (idtoiso_disp (! path_functor_ob p x)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_b p xx) ;; ff ;; 
   idtoiso_disp (path_functor_ob p y)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_f p yy))%mor_disp


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf_functor_disp_mor p ff =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ y ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z] transportf_functor_disp_ob p yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left p f)
  (idtoiso_disp (! path_functor_ob p x)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_b p xx) ;; ff ;; 
   idtoiso_disp (path_functor_ob p y)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_f p yy))%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf_functor_disp_mor (idpath F₁) ff =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob (idpath F₁) xx -->[
   z] transportf_functor_disp_ob (idpath F₁) yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f)
  (idtoiso_disp (! path_functor_ob (idpath F₁) x)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_b (idpath F₁) xx) ;; ff ;; 
   idtoiso_disp (path_functor_ob (idpath F₁) y)
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob_eq_f (idpath F₁) yy))%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
ff =
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f)
  (id_disp xx ;; ff ;; id_disp yy)%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
ff =
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f)
  (transportb (mor_disp xx yy)
     (id_left ((# F₁)%cat f)) ff ;; id_disp yy)%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
ff =
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f)
  (transportb (mor_disp xx yy)
     (id_right (identity (F₁ x) · # F₁ f))
     (transportb (mor_disp xx yy) (id_left (# F₁ f))
        ff))

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
ff =
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f)
  (transportf (mor_disp xx yy)
     (! id_right (identity (F₁ x) · # F₁ f))
     (transportf (mor_disp xx yy) (! id_left (# F₁ f))
        ff))

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
ff =
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (! id_left (# F₁ f) @
   ! id_right (identity (F₁ x) · # F₁ f) @
   path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f) ff

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
transportf (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧, xx -->[ z] yy)
  (! id_left (# F₁ f) @
   ! id_right (identity (F₁ x) · # F₁ f) @
   path_functor_mor_left (idpath F₁) f) ff = ff

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
isaset (C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ y ⟧)

  apply homset_property.
Qed.


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportf_functor_disp_mor p
  (transportb (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
     (functor_id F₁ x) (id_disp xx)) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ x ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z] transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx)
  (functor_id F₂ x)
  (id_disp (transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx))


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportf_functor_disp_mor p
  (transportb (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
     (functor_id F₁ x) (id_disp xx)) =
transportb
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ x ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z] transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx)
  (functor_id F₂ x)
  (id_disp (transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx))

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x: C₁
xx: D (F₁ x)
transportb (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
  (functor_id F₁ x) (id_disp xx) =
transportb (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
  (functor_id F₁ x) (id_disp xx)

  apply idpath.
Qed.


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x, y, z: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
zz: D (F₁ z)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
gg: yy -->[ # F₁ g] zz
transportf_functor_disp_mor p
  (transportb
     (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ z ⟧, xx -->[ z0] zz)
     (functor_comp F₁ f g) (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp) =
transportb
  (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ z ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z0] transportf_functor_disp_ob p zz)
  (functor_comp F₂ f g)
  (transportf_functor_disp_mor p ff ;; transportf_functor_disp_mor
                                         p gg)%mor_disp


C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁, F₂: C₁ ⟶ C₂
p: F₁ = F₂
x, y, z: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
zz: D (F₁ z)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
gg: yy -->[ # F₁ g] zz
transportf_functor_disp_mor p
  (transportb
     (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ z ⟧, xx -->[ z0] zz)
     (functor_comp F₁ f g) (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp) =
transportb
  (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₂ x, F₂ z ⟧,
   transportf_functor_disp_ob p xx -->[
   z0] transportf_functor_disp_ob p zz)
  (functor_comp F₂ f g)
  (transportf_functor_disp_mor p ff ;; transportf_functor_disp_mor
                                         p gg)%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂: category
D: disp_cat C₂
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
x, y, z: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: D (F₁ x)
yy: D (F₁ y)
zz: D (F₁ z)
ff: xx -->[ # F₁ f] yy
gg: yy -->[ # F₁ g] zz
transportb (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ z ⟧, xx -->[ z0] zz)
  (functor_comp F₁ f g) (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportb (λ z0 : C₂ ⟦ F₁ x, F₁ z ⟧, xx -->[ z0] zz)
  (functor_comp F₁ f g) (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp

  apply idpath.
Qed.

(** * 4. The comprehension functor is Cartesian *)
Section ComprehensionPullback.
  Context {G₀ G₁ G₂ : setgroupoid}
          {F : G₁ ⟶ G₂}
          {D : disp_setgrpd G₂}
          (I : cleaving D)
          {H₁ : G₀ ⟶ total_category D}
          {H₂ : G₀ ⟶ G₁}
          (p : H₁ ∙ pr1_category _ = H₂ ∙ F).

  (total_category (reindex_disp_cat F D))

→ total_category (reindex_disp_cat F D) ⟦ ?F a, ?F b ⟧

 exact (λ x, H₂ x ,, transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x))).

→ total_category (reindex_disp_cat F D)
  ⟦ (λ x : G₀,
     H₂ x,, transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x)))
      a,
  (λ x : G₀,
   H₂ x,, transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x))) b
  ⟧
 exact (λ x y f,
             #H₂ f
             ,,
             transportf_functor_disp_mor p (pr2 (#H₁ f))).
  Defined.

          exact (!fiber_paths (!(functor_id H₁ x))).
        
G₀, G₁, G₂: setgroupoid
F: G₁ ⟶ G₂
D: disp_setgrpd G₂
I: cleaving D
H₁: G₀ ⟶ total_category D
H₂: G₀ ⟶ G₁
p: H₁ ∙ pr1_category D = H₂ ∙ F
x: G₀
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x)))
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x))))
  (functor_id H₂ x)
  (transportf_functor_disp_mor p
     (transportf
        (λ x0 : G₂ ⟦ pr1 (H₁ x), pr1 (H₁ x) ⟧,
         pr2 (H₁ x) -->[ x0] pr2 (H₁ x))
        (base_paths (identity (H₁ x))
           (# H₁ (identity x)) (! functor_id H₁ x))
        (pr2 (identity (H₁ x))))) =
transportb
  (mor_disp

  (functor_comp H₂ f g)
  (transportf_functor_disp_mor p
     (transportf
        (λ x0 : G₂ ⟦ pr1 (H₁ x), pr1 (H₁ z) ⟧,
         pr2 (H₁ x) -->[ x0] pr2 (H₁ z))
        (base_paths (# H₁ f · # H₁ g) (# H₁ (f · g))
           (! functor_comp H₁ f g))
        (pr2 (# H₁ f · # H₁ g)))) = ?b

   transportf_functor_disp_mor p (pr2 ((# H₁)%cat g)))%mor_disp

        (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x)))
        (pr2 (pr1 H₁ y)))
     (idtoiso_disp (! path_functor_ob p x)

                                    (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof
                                       y))))%mor_disp) =

G₀, G₁, G₂: setgroupoid
F: G₁ ⟶ G₂
D: disp_setgrpd G₂
I: cleaving D
H₁: G₀ ⟶ total_category D
H₂: G₀ ⟶ G₁
p: H₁ ∙ pr1_category D = H₂ ∙ F
x, y: G₀
f: G₀ ⟦ x, y ⟧
maponpaths (compose (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)))
  (! id_right (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f)) @
maponpaths (compose (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)))
  (maponpaths (compose (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f))
     (! setcategory_refl_idtoiso
          (path_functor_ob p y @
           base_paths
             (F (H₂ y),,
              transportf_functor_disp_ob p
                (pr2 (H₁ y))) (pr1 H₁ y)
             (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof
                y)))) @
maponpaths (compose (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)))
  (maponpaths (compose (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f))
     (pr1_idtoiso_concat (path_functor_ob p y)
        (base_paths
           (F (H₂ y),,
            transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ y)))
           (pr1 H₁ y)
           (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof y)))) @
maponpaths (compose (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)))
  (assoc (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f)
     (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y))
     (pr1
        (idtoiso
           (base_paths
              (F (H₂ y),,
               transportf_functor_disp_ob p
                 (pr2 (H₁ y))) (pr1 H₁ y)
              (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof
                 y))))) @
assoc (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x))
  (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f
   · idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y))
  (pr1
     (idtoiso
        (base_paths
           (F (H₂ y),,
            transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ y)))
           (pr1 H₁ y)
           (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof y)))) @
cancel_postcomposition
  (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)
   · (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f
      · idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y)))
  (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)
   · # (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f
   · idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y))
  (pr1
     (idtoiso
        (base_paths
           (F (H₂ y),,
            transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ y)))
           (pr1 H₁ y)
           (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof y))))
  (assoc (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x))
     (# (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f)
     (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y))) @
cancel_postcomposition
  (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x)
   · # (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f
   · idtoiso (path_functor_ob p y)) (# F (# H₂ f))
  (pr1
     (idtoiso
        (base_paths
           (F (H₂ y),,
            transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ y)))
           (pr1 H₁ y)
           (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof y))))
  (path_functor_mor_left p f) @
isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof0 x y f =
idtoiso_disp_set_grpd_precomp_path
  (! path_functor_ob p x)
  (base_paths
     (F (H₂ x),,
      transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x)))
     (pr1 H₁ x)
     (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_pr1_subproof x))
  (pr1 (# (pr1 H₁) f))

        apply (homset_property G₂).
  Qed.

  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
        (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
     (functor_comp F
        (pr1
           (idtoiso
              (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
                 (H₂ x₁,,
                  transportf_functor_disp_ob p
                    (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
                 (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                    x₁)))) (# H₂ f))
     (pr1 idtoiso_d ;; transportf_functor_disp_mor p
                         (pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f)))%mor_disp) =

  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf_functor_disp_ob p (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (functor_comp F (pr1 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f))
     (pr1
        (idtoiso
           (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
              (H₂ x₂,,
               transportf_functor_disp_ob p
                 (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
              (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                 x₂)))))
  (pr2 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f) ;; pr1 idtoiso_d)%mor_disp

transportb (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (base_paths
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
      (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                               (idtoiso
                                  (path_functor_ob
                                     p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f),,
      (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                                 ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp)
     (path_functor_mor p₁ f))
  (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                              ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp
pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)) = ?y'

              exact (idtoiso_total_category_pr2 (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)).

                                                 f))%mor_disp
transportf
  (λ z : pr1 G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧,
   pr2 (H' x₁) -->[
   z] transportf (pr1 D) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; idtoiso_d)%mor_disp =
(pr2 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f) ;; pr1 idtoiso_d)%mor_disp

                                      p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f0),,

                                                 ((# H₁)%cat

  (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                              ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f0))%mor_disp

· pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂))] pr2
                                           (H₁ x₂)

· idtoiso (maponpaths (λ F : G₀ ⟶ G₂, F x₂) p) =
# F

G₀, G₁, G₂: setgroupoid
F: G₁ ⟶ G₂
D: disp_setgrpd G₂
I: cleaving D
H₁: G₀ ⟶ total_category D
H₂: G₀ ⟶ G₁
p: H₁ ∙ pr1_category D = H₂ ∙ F
H': G₀ ⟶ total_category (reindex_disp_cat F D)
p₁: H'
∙ total_functor
    (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr1 D)) =
H₁
p₂: H' ∙ pr1_category (reindex_disp_cat F (pr1 D)) =
H₂
x₁, x₂: G₀
f: G₀ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
q: (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                         (idtoiso
                            (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp =
transportb (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (base_paths
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
      (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                               (idtoiso
                                  (path_functor_ob
                                     p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f),,
      (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                                 ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp)
     (path_functor_mor p₁ f))
  (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                              ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (transportf
     (λ z : G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧,
      pr2 (H' x₁) -->[
      z] transportf (pr1 D) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
        (base_paths
           ((# F)%cat (pr1 ((# H')%cat f))
            · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
            pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                                    (idtoiso
                                       (path_functor_ob
                                          p₁ x₂)))
           (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
            · pr1 ((# H₁)%cat f),,
            pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; 
            pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f))
           (path_functor_mor p₁ f))
        (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; 
         pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f)) ;; idtoiso_d)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (pr1 idtoiso_d ;; transportf_functor_disp_mor p
                      (pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f)))%mor_disp

        
G₀, G₁, G₂: setgroupoid
F: G₁ ⟶ G₂
D: disp_setgrpd G₂
I: cleaving D

H₂: G₀ ⟶ G₁

H₂
x₁, x₂: G₀
f: G₀ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
q: (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                         (idtoiso
                            (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp =
transportb (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (base_paths
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
      (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                               (idtoiso
                                  (path_functor_ob
                                     p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f),,
      (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                                 ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp)
     (path_functor_mor p₁ f))
  (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                              ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (transportf
     (λ z : pr1 G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧,
      pr2 (H' x₁) -->[
      z] transportf (pr1 D) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
        (base_paths

            · pr1 ((# H₁)%cat f),,
            pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; 
            pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f))

        (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; 
         pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f)) ;; idtoiso_d)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))

                      (pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f)))%mor_disp

    (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr1 D)) =
H₁
p₂: H' ∙ pr1_category (reindex_disp_cat F (pr1 D)) =
H₂
x₁, x₂: G₀
f: G₀ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
q: (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                         (idtoiso
                            (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp =
transportb (mor_disp (pr2 (H' x₁)) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (base_paths
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
      (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                               (idtoiso
                                  (path_functor_ob
                                     p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f),,
      (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                                 ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp)
     (path_functor_mor p₁ f))
  (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; pr2
                                              ((# H₁)%cat
                                                 f))%mor_disp
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
     (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
        (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (pr2 (pr1 H' x₁))
           (transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂))))
        (pr1 idtoiso_d ;; idtoiso_d ;; pr2
                                         ((# H₁)%cat f) ;; idtoiso_d)%mor_disp)) =
transportf
  (λ z : pr1 G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧,
   pr2 (H' x₁) -->[
   z] transportf (pr1 D) (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
  (pr1 idtoiso_d ;; pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f) ;; idtoiso_d)%mor_disp

           (idtoiso
              (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
                 (H₂ x₁,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
                 (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                    x₁)))))
     (idtoiso (! path_functor_ob p x₁)
      · # (H₁ ∙ pr1_category D) f)
     (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p x₂)) @
 maponpaths
   (compose
      (# F
         (pr1
            (idtoiso
               (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
                  (H₂ x₁,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
                  (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                     x₁))))))
   (path_functor_mor_left p f) @
 ! functor_comp F
     (pr1
        (idtoiso
           (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
              (H₂ x₁,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
              (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                 x₁)))) (# H₂ f) @
 maponpaths # F
   (maponpaths_2 compose
      (setcategory_eq_idtoiso
         (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
            (H₂ x₁,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
            (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob x₁))
         (path_functor_ob p₂ x₁)) (# H₂ f) @
    ! path_functor_mor p₂ f @
    maponpaths (compose (pr1 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f)))
      (setcategory_eq_idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₂ x₂)
         (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
            (H₂ x₂,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
            (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob x₂))))) @
! (cancel_postcomposition
     (pr1
        (idtoiso
           (base_paths
              ((H'
                ∙ total_functor
                    (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F
                       (pr1 D))) x₁) (H₁ x₁)
              (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))) · pr1 (# H₁ f))
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f))
     (idtoiso
        (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (pr1
           (idtoiso
              (base_paths
                 ((H'
                   ∙ total_functor
                       (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor
                          F (pr1 D))) x₁) (H₁ x₁)
                 (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))))
        (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)))
        (pr1 (# H₁ f))
        (idtoiso_total_category_pr2_path
           (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
      · pr1 (# H₁ f))
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))
     (idtoiso
        (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p))
     (! base_paths
          (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
           · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)),,
           (pr2 ((# H')%cat f) ;; pr2
                                    (idtoiso
                                       (path_functor_ob
                                          p₁ x₂)))%mor_disp)
          (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
           · pr1 (# H₁ f),,
           (pr2 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁)) ;; 
            pr2 ((# H₁)%cat f))%mor_disp)
          (path_functor_mor p₁ f)) @
   internal_paths_rew_r
     (pr1 G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧)
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂))
      · idtoiso
          (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p))
     (# F (pr1 (# H' f))
      · (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂))
         · idtoiso
             (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂)
                p)))
     (λ p0 : pr1 G₂ ⟦ F (pr1 (H' x₁)), F (H₂ x₂) ⟧,
      p0 =
      # F (pr1 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f))
      · # F
          (pr1
             (idtoiso
                (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
                   (H₂ x₂,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
                   (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                      x₂)))))
     (maponpaths
        (compose (# F (pr1 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f))))
        ((maponpaths_2 compose
            (maponpaths pr1
               (idtoiso_total_category
                  (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))
            (idtoiso
               (maponpaths
                  (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p)) @
          ! pr1_idtoiso_concat
              (base_paths
                 (F (pr1 (H' x₂)),, pr2 (H' x₂))
                 (H₁ x₂) (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂))
              (maponpaths
                 (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p) @
          setcategory_eq_idtoiso
            (base_paths
               (F (pr1 (H' x₂)),, pr2 (H' x₂)) (H₁ x₂)
               (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂) @
             maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂)
               p)
            (maponpaths F
               (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
                  (H₂ x₂,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
                  (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                     x₂)))) @
         pr1_maponpaths_idtoiso F
           (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
              (H₂ x₂,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
              (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                 x₂))))
     (assoc' (# F (pr1 (# H' f)))
        (pr1 (idtoiso (path_functor_ob p₁ x₂)))
        (idtoiso
           (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p))) @
   ! functor_comp F (pr1 ((pr21 H') x₁ x₂ f))
       (pr1
          (idtoiso
             (base_paths (pr1 H' x₂)
                (H₂ x₂,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₂)))
                (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob
                   x₂))))) =
idtoiso_disp_set_grpd_prepostcomp_path
  (maponpaths F
     (base_paths (pr1 H' x₁)
        (H₂ x₁,, transportf D (pr2 (H₁ x₁)))
        (isofib_comprehension_pb_mor_unique_ob x₁)) @
   ! path_functor_ob p x₁)
  (base_paths
     ((H'
       ∙ total_functor
           (reindex_disp_cat_disp_functor F (pr1 D)))
        x₁) (H₁ x₁) (path_functor_ob p₁ x₁))
  (pr1 (# H₁ f)) (path_functor_ob p x₂)
  (maponpaths (λ F : pr1 G₀ ⟶ pr1 G₂, F x₂) p)

        apply (homset_property G₂).
  Qed.
End ComprehensionPullback.

         disp_cat_split_isofib x

 exact (λ (G : setgroupoid)

           ,,
           pr1_category _).
  
(λ Fob : ∏ x : cat_of_setgroupoid,
         disp_cat_split_isofib x
         → disp_codomain cat_of_setgroupoid
             (functor_identity cat_of_setgroupoid x),
 ∏ (x y : cat_of_setgroupoid)

    (total_set_groupoid (pr1 D₂),,

    exact (total_functor_commute_eq (pr11 FF)).
